[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA libFuzzer run against the Apache Commons Compress TAR handling code timed out [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mafter roughly [0m[1;36m28[0m[39m seconds. The thread dump shows the main thread consuming CPU in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJava’s arbitrary-precision division routines [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjava.math.MutableBigInteger.divide* [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand BigDecimal.divide/remainder[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m while parsing decimal-second timestamps in PAX [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheaders via TarArchiveEntry.parseInstantFromDecimalSeconds. This indicates a [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpotential performance hang in the PAX header parsing logic under certain inputs.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue observed  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The fuzzer’s target, CompressTarFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput, invoked the TAR file[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstructor and next-entry retrieval routines.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - libFuzzer reported a timeout [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ERROR: libFuzzer: timeout`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m after about [0m[1;36m27.9[0m[39m s [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof elapsed time.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Thread-dump highlights  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The “main” thread is in state RUNNABLE, spending CPU time in:  [0m                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - These calls originate from:  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - While no explicit CVE or vulnerability classification is given, the symptom is [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma long-running or potentially infinite loop in numeric parsing—a performance or [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdenial-of-service concern.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The harness code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCompressTarFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m merely drives the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibrary; the hang occurs inside Commons Compress.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Decimal-seconds parsing in PAX headers exercises BigDecimal division paths that[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcan be expensive or pathological for certain inputs.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - No crashes or exceptions are shown—only excessive CPU usage leading to a fuzzer[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtimeout.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas for investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m61[0m[39m: * ways, depending on how they are to be used.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m62[0m[39m: * <p>[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m: * TarEntries that are created from the header bytes read from an archive are [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstantiated with the [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m@link TarArchiveEntry#[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbyte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m constructor.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m: * These entries will be used when extracting from or listing the contents of an[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchive. These entries have their header filled in using the header bytes. They[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m65[0m[39m: * also set the File to null, since they reference an archive entry not a file.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m66[0m[39m: * <[0m[35m/[0m[95mp[0m[39m>[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m: * <p>[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m: * TarEntries that are created from Files that are to be written into an archive[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare instantiated with the [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m@link TarArchiveEntry#[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[39mFile[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m or[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m: * [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m@link TarArchiveEntry#[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m constructor. These entries have[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtheir header filled in using the File's information. They also keep a reference[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m: * to the File for convenience when writing entries.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m71[0m[39m: * <[0m[35m/[0m[95mp[0m[39m>[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m72[0m[39m: * <p>[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m73[0m[39m: * Finally, TarEntries can be constructed from nothing but a name. This allows [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe programmer to construct the entry by hand, for instance when only an[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m74[0m[39m: * InputStream is available for writing to the archive, and the header [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minformation is constructed from other information. In this case the header fields [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare set[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m75[0m[39m: * to defaults and the File is set to null.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m76[0m[39m: * <[0m[35m/[0m[95mp[0m[39m>[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m77[0m[39m: * <p>[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m78[0m[39m: * The C structure for a Tar Entry's header is:[0m                                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo prevent pathological BigDecimal division in `parseInstantFromDecimalSeconds` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mand thus avoid DoS via very long decimal‐second strings[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m while preserving existing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPAX header parsing behavior for legitimate timestamps, apply the following patch [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstrategy to the initial codebase in `TarArchiveEntry.java` only:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Tighten the PAX‐time regex  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   In `TarArchiveEntry` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m221[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, change[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     private static final Pattern PAX_EXTENDED_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER_FILE_TIMES_PATTERN =[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mPattern.compile[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"-?\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,19[0m[32m}[0m[32m([0m[32m?:\\.\\d*[0m[32m)[0m[32m?"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   to[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     private static final Pattern PAX_EXTENDED_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER_FILE_TIMES_PATTERN =[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m19[0m[39m integer digits, optional “.” plus up to [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m fractional digits [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mnanosecond precision[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mPattern.compile[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"-?\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,19[0m[32m}[0m[32m([0m[32m?:\\.\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m0,9[0m[32m}[0m[32m)[0m[32m?"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   This immediately rejects any PAX timestamp with more than [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m decimal digits, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbounding the cost of later numeric operations.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Enforce a runtime scale check  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   In `parseInstantFromDecimalSeconds` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m275[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m278[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, after constructing [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe `BigDecimal`, add:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     final BigDecimal epochSeconds = new [0m[1;35mBigDecimal[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvalue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Reject overly precise inputs that pass the regex but still have >[0m[1;36m9[0m[39m [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfractional digits[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mepochSeconds.scale[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m > [0m[1;36m9[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Corrupted PAX header. Too many fractional digits in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mtime field '"[0m[39m + value + [0m[32m"'"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   This secondary check guards against any future regex bypass or manual [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvocation.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Preserve existing behavior  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All valid inputs [0m[1;39m([0m[39mup to nanosecond resolution[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continue to parse via [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mBigDecimal.longValue[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, `[0m[1;35mremainder[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, and `[0m[1;35mmovePointRight[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m9[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` exactly as before.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `DateTimeException` and `ArithmeticException` catch block remains [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged, so out‐of‐range values still yield an I/O error.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. No changes outside `TarArchiveEntry.java`  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not alter fuzzing harness code, utility classes, or external dependencies. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No modifications to tests or other code paths.  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Add targeted unit tests  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - New tests in the existing test suite to assert that:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • A PAX header with exactly [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m fractional digits parses correctly.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • A PAX header with [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m or more fractional digits triggers an `IOException`.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This verifies both the regex and the scale check.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJustification  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The root cause is an unbounded fractional‐digit pattern [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`\\.\\d*`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, allowing [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextremely long decimals that make `BigDecimal.divideAndRemainder` pathological.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Restricting fractional digits to [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m enforces native `Instant` precision, stops [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexcessive CPU usage, and aligns with nanosecond resolution.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The secondary scale check is a defense‐in‐depth to catch any odd edge cases or [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuture code changes that might slip past the regex.  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Existing functionality and valid PAX headers [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwith up to [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m decimal places[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munaffected.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Tests ensure no regressions and explicitly guard the new limit.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPotential Side‐Effects & Mitigations  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Tar files with >[0m[1;36m9[0m[39m fractional digits will now be treated as corrupted rather than [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsed [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpreviously they hung[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Given the lack of a PAX standard on [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marbitrary‐precision fractional seconds, rejecting overly precise values is both [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreasonable and safe.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- If strict backward‐compatibility of exotic PAX headers is required, a future [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39menhancement could truncate rather than reject extra digits, but that can be layered[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mon top of this fundamental DoS fix.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/tar/TarArchiveEntry[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m.jav[0m[1;92ma:220[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m223[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/tar/TarArchiveEntry[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m.jav[0m[1;92ma:274[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m278[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
